The mechanics here are good people. I've been taking my Volvo S40 there for over 3 years. They do quality repairs with fair prices. They have been nothing but helpful and kind. Nate always explains the car problem in terms that I understand and shows me the parts that were replaced. When I'm tight on money he lets me know what needs to be done now and what can wait plus they offer carecredit to help with the payments. When I had an accident and other person's insurance provided me with a rental car Orr dealt with the rental company regarding how long I would need the rental for. He also advised me on how to deal with the guy that hit me because he just wanted to give me cash instead of go through his insurance. Nate advised against that and thank goodness because the cost of the damages were WAY more than the guy was offering. That's just a few of the many ways that he has helped me out over the years.

I would recommend this auto shop to anyone that wants an honest mechanic with quality service at an affordable price.<//text>

<Text>While visiting friends in Montclair, my wife's Toyota Matrix started leaking under the dash (on her new suede shoes!). We weren't excited about the idea of another breakdown driving from Southern to Northern California, but neither were we excited about going to an unfamiliar mechanic. After research, we found ourselves at Orr Automotive and we're super glad we did.

John treated us right. He walked us through the steps of his diagnosis, took us out to the car to show us his findings, and gave us a discount on additional issues he found 'since he was digging around anyway.' Chris treated us well, too, driving us back to our spot and chatting us up about auto maintenance tips and life in Montclair.

< text>
It is so nice to have a brewery in the neighborhood!  Their beers are delicious, the food is great, the atmosphere is welcoming, and even when it's busy, the wait isn't terribly long.  Last time I was there it did take a little longer than usual to get food, but it was pretty packed.  Everything came out piping hot and delicious, though, and was definitely worth the wait.  They also have growlers for $8, which is the cheapest I've seen the glass sold for, and the fill prices are totally reasonable.  It's great to be able to take it home!< /text>

<UserId.>109195705425644993412</UserId.><Name>Robert M</Name><date>1591481321216< /date><rate>1< /rate>< review>
I had my car checked by them so it's standard procedure for repair shops like this to charge you a diagnostic fee for finding out the problem of your vehicle. I left my car for I have to go to work and an employee named Peter who seems to be a nice trustworthy guy and an amicable person will call me on what they find wrong with it. Peter calls me back later in the day and tells me what's wrong with my car. To make sure I asked Peter if I he can waive the $132 diagnostic fee if I agree to have my car fixed at their shop. He exactly relied YES and so I agreed to have them work on my car and repair it it to have it in good running condition.

I came back the next morning to pick up my car and pay for the bill. Everything was fine at that point and I went on my way to work. I was about a mile away when I saw the on my bill that the diagnostic fee wasn't waived at all so I went back to talk about out conversation from yesterday about the fee.

So I showed him on the invoice the diagnostic fee and asked why he charged me when we agreed in our phone conversation the day before that it will be waived. Alas he replied to me that he never agreed on the waiver and he doesn't remember that we talked about it in our conversation. I didn't bother to press my point anymore for I am sure I will be wasting my time on a pointless discussion about the fee and just left. Be aware that they will charge you a $132 diagnostic fee even if you have your car repaired at their shop as per company policy which is a rip-off if you ask me.

In all my experience having my vehicle repaired at several repair shops already Sunland is the only shop that charges a diagnostic fee only. Now it is standard operating procedure for a repair shop to waive the diagnostic fee once you agreed to have your vehicle be repaired at their establishment. Even the big companies like Toyota or Ford car dealership have the same system.

Sunland has lost my business because of this BS and even though I still need repairs done to my car, I will never come back to them ever. Be smart and stay away from them.< /review>

< review>
First off as I was making my way through Ulta store @ 7000 Market Pl Dr, Goleta, CA 93117 between 12pm-1:30pm on 1/26/18 I was appalled at over hearing a store associate speaking negatively about customers within ear shot of myself shopping the store. It was awkward & uncomfortable to say the least. The associate that was gripping about customers stating that she can't get anything done because a customer will walk up and start moving display items around again this person was Deborah at least that is what she stated her name is, but she as well as a few others were not wearing name badges. She is tall, Caucasian, about late 40's, 50 or 60, medium length dark brown/black hair, severe red lipstick on. She did approach me to ask if I needed help, and that seemed insincere especially after hearing her speech beforehand. I said I am looking for an eyeliner by Ulta, and I was in front of Ulta products to which she made it seem like I was well equipped after finding Ulta brand she slyly distanced herself from me. Her co-worker whom she was complaining to however stepped in shortly after Deborah departed. Allie asked if I needed help, I told her yes I am looking for an Ulta duo eyeliner, and Allie actually remembered the product & explained it is a seasonal item then she went on to see if she could find me the plum shade I fell in love with. We both searched and found Mystic Ulta eyeliner to be the best match. I thanked her and continued shopping. I then was trying to find a lip scrub, and was guided by another friendly associate to Pacifica brand lip scrub.  I thanked her and tried the lip scrub out on my wrist and carefully chose the lip item in front that were all opened. As I was testing what clearly was a used Test item, that is when Deborah decided I need a stern talking to. She said I am not allowed to try items on, and I said it is a tester & has already clearly been used many times as such. She snottily said it will say tester on it if it is a tester. I then asked her name, and pointed out that she should then remove all the items in the front that have been opened so no one else buys them and or mistakenly uses them as a tester. She said well then we wouldn't be able to sell them....I was shocked! She clearly could see & I pointed out all the lip items in the front display were all opened way before I got there & all were clearly being used as testers!!! So for her to attack me for not doing her job was quite the opposite of the very Top notch service I always get from Ulta. I got the feeling she doesn't even like her job or customers, and though I had my hands clearly full of items I happily found to purchase she treated me like an unwelcome customer as she clearly can't stand any of us a she stated earlier to her co-worker. So, I get that she hates her job & customers but don't feel she had the right to take out her aggression on me. I have never ever been so aggressively approached by any customer service person Ever!  I am happy to say that this kind of customer service is not my normal experience, and I left happy with the items I was able to find. I am however still horrified that she did not remove the items from the Pacifica line that were all open and being used as testers! That means she will knowingly allow her co-workers to sell used items, and let customers buy from items that were already used in store!</review>

<text>My experience at the hair salon was sub-par.

The reason I decided to try the hair salon at Ulta was because I received via mail a coupon for a $30 cut and style for new guests. It said to book online by 4/19/2017. On Wednesday the 19th, I didn't have access to wifi, so I called and made an appointment over the phone. The woman I spoke to said there were no walk-ins available for that day, so I made one for 1 o'clock the next day (Thursday).

When I arrived Thursday at 1, there was no one at the salon counter. After waiting a few moments, I went in search of an employee. The store was nearly empty, so I found one immediately. She directed me to Cecilia, who was to be my stylist. Cecilia acknowledged me then promptly walked away with some guy she had been talking to. I continued to wait at the salon bar for an extra 5-10 minutes while various other employees asked me if I had an appointment and didn't seem to know where Cecilia had gone. This all happened while on my lunch break, so I was under a time constraint.

Strangely, it wasn't until 3:54 pm that same day that I received a text confirming my appointment at 1 pm. A miscommunication about appointments is  understandable, but I found Cecilia's behavior to be unprofessional.

Additionally, I was not very satisfied with the haircut she gave. I asked for layers and a trim - I said that I don't mind sacrificing a bit of length if it makes my ends look healthier. But after she was finished, I had to ask her to go over certain spots again, because there were still lots of noticeable split ends. She also didn't cut the hair framing my face at all until I specifically requested.

My hair also felt very dry after the blowout. I was curious about the products she used. She used Redken anti-frizz shampoo, which I don't feel was very appropriate for my hair type. I'm not sure what hairspray she used (she wasn't sure when I asked), but it didn't seem to have any heat protective elements. My hair felt damaged after the blowout.

And finally, she was very rough with the way she handled my hair. She neglected to brush out any of the tangles after washing my hair, so each time she made a long pass with the comb, it ripped out some of my baby hairs. I could see them knotted in the comb after she was finished. I'm not usually tender headed, but that hurt.

Disappointingly, I forgot to bring the coupon with me to my appointment, so I paid full price for this negative experience.< /text><Pictures>None<//Pictures>< Response>

<review>Moderate to strenuous trail to the highest spot in the Santa Monica Mountains (3133ft elevation). There‚Äôs free parking available if you input Sandstone Peak trailhead. You could also park at the Mishe Mowka trailhead but that lot was a bit smaller and had more people. There are two bathrooms available at the Sandstone trailhead. You can opt to go clockwise for a shorter but steeper ascent, or counterclockwise for a longer but more gradual ascent. The trail connects to others like the Secret Grotto and the Balanced Rock trail. Note that the latter is a trail that‚Äôs not maintained by the NPS so it‚Äôs overgrown.

The trail is rocky and to get up to the peak, you might need to strategically rock climb (in the loosest sense). Wear hiking boots, sneakers work give you good traction. There‚Äôs little shade so wear sunscreen and bring a hat. Dogs are allowed on the trail. No permits are required to hike. You‚Äôll most likely not have signal so bring a map / check the trail beforehand. Overall, the trail provides a great workout and the opportunity to enjoy some fresh air away from the crowds.< /review><pictures>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipMhBUYgv__ZUECMxKPVz1ooE8td_nJnqRCU3v7X=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipP4pkKYb6A0TbAFbwCVK1MSHrQ7FXczA63E4SLy=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipNCjLkZbozpx2_sBjTe3SGUX2DUPx7EBNo86AC4=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipN6SrPALaETpODs3zKO3plfyaA0VR6y3RGO0rIe=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipNptcSBlU--3HrgLXDJfcDoKiw2dal282TG5Gwh=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipN8kJ6376ztVrh1S5w0Ws8jZrbgSg5bvXVxJ4bV=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipMn3SAZLKY-1FSjpdZl16m37Tkekpe8Mma8ZdoA=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipPX3YkzKFYMTdZMhAMEu6b2SkedmafBNTxqGmOf=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipMxsedvpw9gl55i1iONOA7kE2ypEctbS27K7UWX=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipM8CNtivU3v_DOxMTFhByS9C2AOmzk3TPHHqhF9=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipNINmrKn-TNUJN6TYZnoEeNqHK9qkyd9JEBRi9q=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipN2iJ4Bgiz7rjVs0gotQxBNrEd9JXD-_FM0yaXD=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipPtUtQguXtG7G4Bd6hkQeMq6xchaIdUlAgyoWaR=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipPn2MjrBVYTnPgJwSypkRJsi-aVIM4gaygOGFba=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]</pictures>< resp>

<review>This hike was awesome. We took the more aggressive 3 mile loop because we were a little short on time. Round trip with a 20 minute stop at the top took us about 2.5 hours. <name>Vic Hanson<//name><Review>Sandstone Peak is the highest point in the Santa Monica Mountains and gives some good views. There are two nearby parking lots off of Yerba Buena Road, the Sandstone Peak Trailhead and the Mishe Mokwa Trailhead. The distance is similar from either one. There are a number of trails but they are fairly well marked but a map can be helpful. The Backbone Trail goes near the Sandsone Peak TH but passes right through the Mishe Mokwa TH. Two other interesting side hikes go to the Grotto (starts across the road from Sandstone TH) and Balance Rock, which is a side trail easily accessed from either TH. It is easy to make a loop hike using the other trails. The Grotto has a nice little pool hidden down among large boulders and Balance Rock is a huge rock standing on top of one on ground level. It is amazing that the earthquakes haven't toppled it!< /Review><Time>1604968869161<//Time>< pics>

< Review>
My all time favorite hike in LA and surrounding counties. This is the tallest peak of the Santa Monica Mountain range, what more do I need to say? The whole loop trail is just around 6 miles total, and it is beautiful every step of the way. You start at a very tall elevation, so you get amazing views right from the start. It goes from canyon views, to a balanced rock on a cliff, to the staircase leading up to the monument, reminding you that you have reached the top. The views are spectacular in any direction that you look. On a clear day, you could see as far down as Ventura on the right, and the entire Santa Monica - Long Beach coastline. It is a challenge but no too difficult, so take anyone that hasn't experienced a hike like this before!<//Review>

<Review>One of the most beautiful hikes in the Santa Monica Mountains.

Voted as the best hike in LA by the Modern Hiker.

Beautiful hike....great rock landscapes; great photo ops.

Trails can be very rocky.

Pack water & keep hydrated. =)

Peak Distance: 6-mile loop.

Hiking Time: 5 hours

Elevation Gain: 1100 feet.

Difficulty: Moderate - Strenuous

SOME OF THE KEY POINTS OF INTEREST you will SEE ALONG THE HIKE:

Inspiration Point - here there is a journal that visitors can sign
Balanced Rock
Split Rock
Climbing Walls
Tri-Peaks
Views of Los Angeles, including Catalina Island, Pacific Coast, Channel Islands (on a clear day)

Bring plenty water, snacks, comfy walking/hiking shoes, hat & sunscreen.< /Review><pictures>None< /pictures><Time>1425894813527<//Time></record>

<UserId.>114884144397845288655< /UserId.><time>1375483474284< /time><GmapID>0x80e83b92592187f1:0xd4455f19e188b390<//GmapID>< rating>

< Review>
One of the best hikes in the Santa Monica mountains and even the rest of LA. A fork about 1/2 mile in lets you pick a longer loop (approx. 6.5 miles), or a shorter out and back route (3 miles) that leads to the tallest mountain in Malibu. As you climb, you go through some scenic valleys, shaded tunnels underneath trees, and scenic overlooks offering views of the Conejo Valley.

At the top you'll find a small plaque dedicated to William Allen, a Boy Scout and namesake of the mountain (Sandstone Peak is also called Mt. Allen) and 360 degree views over Malibu, the Pacific Ocean and the Conejo Valley. On clear days you can even see all the way down to Oxnard and Ventura.

The other bonus is it's not too crowded compared to some other Malibu-area hikes, like Escondido Falls.<//Review>
< Name>
Christopher Mejia<//Name>

Dave in the Service Dept. was very nice, knowledgeable and helpful.  Downside was bike was not ready for several weeks after being promised to be ready in 4-5 business days. 113046386628652980402</user_id>
<user_name>Kedar Shah< /user_name><time>1615760610379<//time><rate>5</rate>< Text>
Saturday morning veggie and fruit market with good selection of standard, asian, Indian, south east asian veggies. Was able to find some unique items like methi (fenugreek leaves), arbi, karela (bitter gourd), saag (mustard greens), etc. One of the stalls is family run (Lee farms) and will do special orders if you ask them in advance. I was able to get a large batch of full lemongrass plants and leaves. Only one of the stalls is certified organic and has a wide range of vegetables. Fresh egg vendor, a couple stalls that sell small plants and orchids, and one stall that sells local honey. Great spot to get seasonal fresh items. Check it out!</Text>

<rating>5</rating>< Text>
Really nice place to pick up your vegetables and stuff on a Saturday. SATURDAY ONLY! They have everything from fruits to bread to vegetables to organic eggs. Asian vegetables like bok choy and yuchoi here are much nicer than what you will find in asian markets. Come early for the best items! Parking is a bit rough , try to park around Millbrae avenue< /Text>

<rate>3<//rate>< text>
Fantastic customer service from the ladies at the register. It was our first visit and they took the time to explain the ordering and make recommendations. They use peanut oil and have bins of free peanuts to snack on which is a nice touch.

The restaurant is new and pretty clean. The bathrooms were spotless. It wasn't too busy at lunch on a Saturday, and the wait for food was only about five minutes.

The fries are delicious and come out piping hot! They are heavy handed with the salt, so if you're sensitive you may want to make a special request.

My daughter loved the plain ketchup hot dog. My husband had a bacon burger with mushrooms that was great. My cheeseburger was just ok. The meat patty was well seasoned and it came out hot. My complaint is there was only a scant bit of BBQ sauce. I had to look to see if it was added because I didn't taste it in the first bite, so only 3-stars for now.<//text>

< Text>
This was my first visit to this burger chain that has seemingly unseated In-n-out as the nations most popular.
The service was great. The young lady that helped us was patient in explaining the menu board, so we were able to make a choice.
I chose to have my burger the same way I get it from In-n-out so I could easily compare.
The good thing about Five guys, even though it's a little more expensive is that the burger is more substantial and therefore I felt more satisfied.
And it was a tasty burger (read that with Sam Jackson's voice in mind).  And I also think I might like the fries better.
But to be honest, the In-n-out burger is more flavorful. In-n-out actually makes you want another burger, which is a good strategy.
But the Five Guys burger makes you feel like you wanna come back...on another day.
And I will be back.
But, no offense to this particular location, I'm still a In-n-out guy.</Text>
